[.text-message+&amp;]:mt-1"><div class="flex w-full flex-col gap-1 empty:hidden items-end rtl:items-start"><div class="user-message-bubble-color corner-superellipse/0.98 relative rounded-[22px] px-4 py-2.5 leading-6 max-w-(--user-chat-width,70%)"><div class="whitespace-pre-wrap">DROP TABLE IF EXISTS retail_sales;

CREATE TABLE retail_sales
(
    transactions_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    sale_date DATE,	
    sale_time TIME,
    customer_id INT,	
    gender VARCHAR(10),
    age INT,
    category VARCHAR(35),
    quantity INT,
    price_per_unit FLOAT,	
    cogs FLOAT,
    total_sale FLOAT
);

SELECT * 
FROM retail_sales
LIMIT 100;

--NULL VALUES
SELECT *
FROM retail_sales
WHERE 	transactions_id IS NULL
		OR
		sale_date IS NULL
		OR
		sale_time IS NULL
		OR
		gender IS NULL
		OR
		age IS NULL
		OR
		category IS NULL
		OR
		quantity IS NULL
		OR
		cogs IS NULL
		OR
		total_sale IS NULL
;

--DELETE NULL ROWS
DELETE FROM
retail_sales
WHERE 	transactions_id IS NULL
		OR
		sale_date IS NULL
		OR
		sale_time IS NULL
		OR
		gender IS NULL
		OR
		age IS NULL
		OR
		category IS NULL
		OR
		quantity IS NULL
		OR
		cogs IS NULL
		OR
		total_sale IS NULL
;


SELECT COUNT(*)
FROM retail_sales;

--Important questions
-- Q.1 Write a SQL query to retrieve all columns for sales made on '2022-11-05
SELECT *
FROM retail_sales
WHERE sale_date = '2022-11-05';

-- Q.2 Write a SQL query to retrieve all transactions where the category is 'Clothing' and the quantity sold is more than 3 in the month of Nov-2022
SELECT *
FROM retail_sales
WHERE category = 'Clothing'
AND quantity  &gt; 3
AND   TO_CHAR(sale_date,'YYYY-MM') = '2022-11';


-- Q.3 Write a SQL query to calculate the total sales (total_sale) for each category.
SELECT category,
       SUM(total_sale) AS Total_sale
FROM retail_sales
GROUP BY category
ORDER BY SUM(total_sale);

-- Q.4 Write a SQL query to find the average age of customers who purchased items from the 'Beauty' category.
SELECT ROUND(AVG(age),3) AS age
FROM retail_sales
WHERE category = 'Beauty';


-- Q.5 Write a SQL query to find all transactions where the total_sale is greater than 1000.

SELECT transactions_id,
	   total_sale
FROM retail_sales
WHERE total_sale &gt;1000;

-- Q.6 Write a SQL query to find the total number of transactions (transaction_id) made by each gender in each category.
SELECT COUNT(*) AS No_of_transactions,
	   gender,
	   category
FROM retail_sales
GROUP BY gender,category;	 

-- Q.7 Write a SQL query to calculate the average sale for each month. Find out best selling month in each year
SELECT *
FROM(
		SELECT EXTRACT(YEAR FROM sale_date) AS Year,
			   EXTRACT(MONTH FROM sale_date) AS Month,
			   AVG(total_sale) AS Average_sale,
			   RANK () OVER(PARTITION BY EXTRACT(YEAR FROM sale_date)ORDER BY  AVG(total_sale) DESC) AS rank
			
		FROM  retail_sales
		GROUP BY Year,Month
		) AS t
WHERE rank =1;


-- Q.8 Write a SQL query to find the top 5 customers based on the highest total sales 

SELECT customer_id,
	   SUM(total_sale) AS Total_sale
FROM retail_sales
GROUP BY customer_id
ORDER BY Total_sale DESC
LIMIT 5;

-- Q.9 Write a SQL query to find the number of unique customers who purchased items from each category.
SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT customer_id) AS No_of_customers,
	   category
FROM retail_sales
GROUP BY category;

-- Q.10 Write a SQL query to create each shift and number of orders (Example Morning &lt;=12, Afternoon Between 12 &amp; 17, Evening &gt;17)
WITH hourly_sales
AS (
		SELECT * ,
		CASE 
			WHEN EXTRACT(HOUR FROM sale_time) &lt;12  THEN 'Morning'
			WHEN EXTRACT(HOUR FROM sale_time) BETWEEN 12 AND 17  THEN 'Aternoon'
			ELSE 'Evening'
		END AS shift
			
			
		
		FROM retail_sales
)
SELECT 	shift,
		COUNT(*) AS total_orders
FROM hourly_sales
GROUP  BY shift;

<hr data-start="114" data-end="117">
<h1 data-start="119" data-end="162">🛒 Retail Sales SQL Data Analysis Project</h1>
<h2 data-start="164" data-end="186">📌 Project Overview</h2>
<p data-start="188" data-end="422">This project focuses on analyzing retail sales data using <strong data-start="246" data-end="253">SQL</strong>.<br data-start="254" data-end="257">
The objective is to clean the dataset, explore key business questions, and generate insights related to sales performance, customer behavior, and product categories.</p>
<p data-start="424" data-end="519">This project demonstrates practical SQL skills required for a <strong data-start="486" data-end="507">Data Analyst role</strong>, including:</p>
<ul data-start="521" data-end="644">
<li data-start="521" data-end="536">
<p data-start="523" data-end="536">Data Cleaning</p>
</li>
<li data-start="537" data-end="555">
<p data-start="539" data-end="555">Data Exploration</p>
</li>
<li data-start="556" data-end="570">
<p data-start="558" data-end="570">Aggregations</p>
</li>
<li data-start="571" data-end="581">
<p data-start="573" data-end="581">Grouping</p>
</li>
<li data-start="582" data-end="600">
<p data-start="584" data-end="600">Window Functions</p>
</li>
<li data-start="601" data-end="610">
<p data-start="603" data-end="610">Ranking</p>
</li>
<li data-start="611" data-end="644">
<p data-start="613" data-end="644">Common Table Expressions (CTEs)</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="646" data-end="649">
<h2 data-start="651" data-end="676">🗂 Dataset Information</h2>
<p data-start="678" data-end="704">Table Name: <code data-start="690" data-end="704">retail_sales</code></p>
<h3 data-start="706" data-end="728">📊 Table Structure</h3>

<h2 data-start="1872" data-end="1912">📈 Business Questions &amp; SQL Solutions</h2>
<h3 data-start="1914" data-end="1947">🔹 Q1: Sales on Specific Date</h3>
<p data-start="1948" data-end="1990">Retrieve all sales made on <strong data-start="1975" data-end="1989">2022-11-05</strong>.</p>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="1992" data-end="2061"><div class="relative w-full mt-4 mb-1"><div class=""><div class="relative"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0" style="width: 100%; margin-bottom: calc(-4px); height: calc(4px); mask-image: linear-gradient(transparent 25%, white 75%);"><div class="sticky bg-token-border-light" style="top: calc(var(--sticky-padding-top) + 48px); height: 1px;"></div></div></div><div class="" style="transform: none;"><div class="relative z-0 flex max-w-full"><div id="code-block-viewer" dir="ltr" class="q9tKkq_viewer cm-editor z-10 light:cm-light dark:cm-light flex h-full w-full flex-col items-stretch ͼk ͼy"><div class="cm-scroller"><div class="cm-content q9tKkq_readonly"><span class="ͼn">SELECT</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">*</span><br><span class="ͼn">FROM</span><span> retail_sales</span><br><span class="ͼn">WHERE</span><span> sale_date </span><span class="ͼn">=</span><span> </span><span class="ͼr">'2022-11-05'</span><span>;</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=""><div class="" style="width: 100%; <h3 data-start="2068" data-end="2118">🔹 Q2: Clothing Sales (Nov 2022, Quantity &gt; 3)</h3>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="2120" data-end="2248"><div class="relative w-full mt-4 mb-1"><div class=""><div class="relative"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0" style="width: 100%; margin-bottom: calc(-4px); height: calc(4px); mask-image: linear-gradient(transparent 25%, white 75%);"><div class="sticky bg-token-border-light" style="top: calc(var(--sticky-padding-top) + 48px); height: 1px;"></div></div></div><div class="" style="transform: none;"><div class="relative z-0 flex max-w-full"><div id="code-block-viewer" dir="ltr" class="q9tKkq_viewer cm-editor z-10 light:cm-light dark:cm-light flex h-full w-full flex-col items-stretch ͼk ͼy"><div class="cm-scroller"><div class="cm-content q9tKkq_readonly"><span class="ͼn">SELECT</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">*</span><br><span class="ͼn">FROM</span><span> retail_sales</span><br><span class="ͼn">WHERE</span><span> category </span><span class="ͼn">=</span><span> </span><span class="ͼr">'Clothing'</span><br><span class="ͼn">AND</span><span> quantity </span><span class="ͼn">&gt;</span><span> </span><span class="ͼq">3</span><br><span class="ͼn">AND</span><span> TO_CHAR(sale_date,</span><span class="ͼr">'YYYY-MM'</span><span>) </span><span class="ͼn">=</span><span> </span><span class="ͼr">'2022-11'</span><span>;</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=""><div class="" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"></div></div></div></div></div></pre>

margin-bottom: calc(-4px); height: calc(4px); mask-image: linear-gradient(transparent 25%, white 75%);"><div class="sticky bg-token-border-light" style="top: calc(var(--sticky-padding-top) + 48px); height: 1px;"></div></div></div><div class="" style="transform: none;"><div class="relative z-0 flex max-w-full"><div id="code-block-viewer" dir="ltr" class="q9tKkq_viewer cm-editor z-10 light:cm-light dark:cm-light flex h-full w-full flex-col items-stretch ͼk ͼy"><div class="cm-scroller"><div class="cm-content q9tKkq_readonly"><span class="ͼn">SELECT</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">COUNT</span><span>(</span><span class="ͼn">*</span><span>) </span><span class="ͼn">AS</span><span> No_of_transactions,</span><br><span>       gender,</span><br><span>       category</span><br><span class="ͼn">FROM</span><span> retail_sales</span><br><span class="ͼn">GROUP</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">BY</span><span> gender, category;</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=""><div class="" style="width: 100%; <h3 data-start="2905" data-end="2965">🔹 Q7: Best Selling Month in Each Year (Window Function)</h3>
<p data-start="2967" data-end="2983">This query uses:</p>
<ul data-start="2985" data-end="3045">
<li data-start="2985" data-end="2998">
<p data-start="2987" data-end="2998"><code data-start="2987" data-end="2998">EXTRACT()</code></p>
</li>
<li data-start="2999" data-end="3008">
<p data-start="3001" data-end="3008"><code data-start="3001" data-end="3008">AVG()</code></p>
</li>
<li data-start="3009" data-end="3026">
<p data-start="3011" data-end="3026"><code data-start="3011" data-end="3026">RANK() OVER()</code></p>
</li>
<li data-start="3027" data-end="3045">
<p data-start="3029" data-end="3045">Window Functions</p>
</li>
</ul>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="3047" data-end="3435"><div class="relative w-full mt-4 mb-1"><div class=""><div class="relative"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"><div class="border border-token-border-light border-radius-3xl corner-superellipse/1.1 rounded-3xl"><div class="h-full w-full border-radius-3xl bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary corner-superellipse/1.1 overflow-clip rounded-3xl lxnfua_clipPathFallback"><div class="sticky z-2 select-none top-(--sticky-padding-top)"><div class="flex w-full items-center justify-between py-1.5 ps-4 pe-1.5 font-sans md:ps-5 bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary"><div class="flex max-w-[75%] min-w-0 cursor-default items-center text-sm font-medium justify-self-start text-token-text-primary"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm me-2.5 shrink-0"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-fk4oovux.svg#e45ab3" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>SQL</div><div class="flex flex-row items-center gap-0.5 justify-self-end"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-2 text-sm font-medium hover:bg-black/5 dark:hover:bg-white/10 size-9 rounded-full px-2" aria-label="Copy" data-state="closed"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-md"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-fk4oovux.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg></button></div></div></div><div class="pointer-events-none absolute inset-x-4 top-12 bottom-4"><div class="pointer-events-none sticky z-40 shrink-0 z-1!" style="top: calc(calc(var(--sticky-padding-top) + 48px) - 1px * 3); margin-bottom: calc(-4px); height: calc(4px); mask-image: linear-gradient(transparent 25%, white 75%);"><div class="sticky bg-token-border-light" style="top: calc(var(--sticky-padding-top) + 48px); height: 1px;"></div></div></div><div class="" style="transform: none;"><div class="relative z-0 flex max-w-full"><div id="code-block-viewer" dir="ltr" class="q9tKkq_viewer cm-editor z-10 light:cm-light dark:cm-light flex h-full w-full flex-col items-stretch ͼk ͼy"><div class="cm-scroller"><div class="cm-content q9tKkq_readonly"><span class="ͼn">SELECT</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">*</span><br><span class="ͼn">FROM</span><span>(</span><br><span>    </span><span class="ͼn">SELECT</span><span> EXTRACT(</span><span class="ͼn">YEAR</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">FROM</span><span> sale_date) </span><span class="ͼn">AS</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">Year</span><span>,</span><br><span>           EXTRACT(</span><span class="ͼn">MONTH</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">FROM</span><span> sale_date) </span><span class="ͼn">AS</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">Month</span><span>,</span><br><span>           AVG(total_sale) </span><span class="ͼn">AS</span><span> Average_sale,</span><br><span>           RANK() OVER(</span><br><span>                PARTITION </span><span class="ͼn">BY</span><span> EXTRACT(</span><span class="ͼn">YEAR</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">FROM</span><span> sale_date)</span><br><span>                </span><span class="ͼn">ORDER</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">BY</span><span> AVG(total_sale) </span><span class="ͼn">DESC</span><br><span>           ) </span><span class="ͼn">AS</span><span> rank</span><br><span>    </span><span class="ͼn">FROM</span><span> retail_sales</span><br><span>    </span><span class="ͼn">GROUP</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">BY</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">Year</span><span>, </span><span class="ͼn">Month</span><br><span>) </span><span class="ͼn">AS</span><span> t</span><br><span class="ͼn">WHERE</span><span> rank </span><span class="ͼn">=</span><span> </span><span class="ͼq">1</span><span>;</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=""><div class="" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"></div></div></div></div></div></pre>

<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="3485" data-end="3625"><div class="relative w-full mt-4 mb-1"><div class=""><div class="relative"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0" style="width: 100%; margin-bottom: calc(-4px); height: calc(4px); mask-image: linear-gradient(transparent 25%, white 75%);"><div class="sticky bg-token-border-light" style="top: calc(var(--sticky-padding-top) + 48px); height: 1px;"></div></div></div><div class="" style="transform: none;"><div class="relative z-0 flex max-w-full"><div id="code-block-viewer" dir="ltr" class="q9tKkq_viewer cm-editor z-10 light:cm-light dark:cm-light flex h-full w-full flex-col items-stretch ͼk ͼy"><div class="cm-scroller"><div class="cm-content q9tKkq_readonly"><span class="ͼn">SELECT</span><span> customer_id,</span><br><span>       SUM(total_sale) </span><span class="ͼn">AS</span><span> Total_sale</span><br><span class="ͼn">FROM</span><span> retail_sales</span><br><span class="ͼn">GROUP</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">BY</span><span> customer_id</span><br><span class="ͼn">ORDER</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">BY</span><span> Total_sale </span><span class="ͼn">DESC</span><br><span class="ͼn">LIMIT</span><span> </span><span class="ͼq">5</span><span>;</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=""><div class="" style="width: 100%; <h3 data-start="3632" data-end="3671">🔹 Q9: Unique Customers by Category</h3>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="3673" data-end="3791"><div class="relative w-full mt-4 mb-1"><div class=""><div class="relative"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0" style="width: 100%; margin-bottom: calc(-4px); height: calc(4px); mask-image: linear-gradient(transparent 25%, white 75%);"><div class="sticky bg-token-border-light" style="top: calc(var(--sticky-padding-top) + 48px); height: 1px;"></div></div></div><div class="" style="transform: none;"><div class="relative z-0 flex max-w-full"><div id="code-block-viewer" dir="ltr" class="q9tKkq_viewer cm-editor z-10 light:cm-light dark:cm-light flex h-full w-full flex-col items-stretch ͼk ͼy"><div class="cm-scroller"><div class="cm-content q9tKkq_readonly"><span class="ͼn">SELECT</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">COUNT</span><span>(</span><span class="ͼn">DISTINCT</span><span> customer_id) </span><span class="ͼn">AS</span><span> No_of_customers,</span><br><span>       category</span><br><span class="ͼn">FROM</span><span> retail_sales</span><br><span class="ͼn">GROUP</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">BY</span><span> category;</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=""><div class="" style="width: 100%; <h3 data-start="3798" data-end="3847">🔹 Q10: Sales by Shift (CTE + CASE Statement)</h3>
<p data-start="3849" data-end="3870">Shift Classification:</p>
<ul data-start="3871" data-end="3932">
<li data-start="3871" data-end="3892">
<p data-start="3873" data-end="3892">Morning → Hour &lt; 12</p>
</li>
<li data-start="3893" data-end="3915">
<p data-start="3895" data-end="3915">Afternoon → 12 to 17</p>
</li>
<li data-start="3916" data-end="3932">
<p data-start="3918" data-end="3932">Evening → &gt; 17</p>
</li>
</ul>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="3934" data-end="4294"><div class="relative w-full mt-4 mb-1"><div class=""><div class="relative"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"><div class="border border-token-border-light border-radius-3xl corner-superellipse/1.1 rounded-3xl"><div class="h-full w-full border-radius-3xl bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary corner-superellipse/1.1 overflow-clip rounded-3xl lxnfua_clipPathFallback"><div class="sticky z-2 select-none top-(--sticky-padding-top)"><div class="flex w-full items-center justify-between py-1.5 ps-4 pe-1.5 font-sans md:ps-5 bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary"><div class="flex max-w-[75%] min-w-0 cursor-default items-center text-sm font-medium justify-self-start text-token-text-primary"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm me-2.5 shrink-0"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-fk4oovux.svg#e45ab3" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>SQL</div><div class="flex flex-row items-center gap-0.5 justify-self-end"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-2 text-sm font-medium hover:bg-black/5 dark:hover:bg-white/10 size-9 rounded-full px-2" aria-label="Copy" data-state="closed"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-md"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-fk4oovux.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg></button></div></div></div><div class="pointer-events-none absolute inset-x-4 top-12 bottom-4"><div class="pointer-events-none sticky z-40 shrink-0 z-1!" style="top: calc(calc(var(--sticky-padding-top) + 48px) - 1px * 3); margin-bottom: calc(-4px); height: calc(4px); mask-image: linear-gradient(transparent 25%, white 75%);"><div class="sticky bg-token-border-light" style="top: calc(var(--sticky-padding-top) + 48px); height: 1px;"></div></div></div><div class="" style="transform: none;"><div class="relative z-0 flex max-w-full"><div id="code-block-viewer" dir="ltr" class="q9tKkq_viewer cm-editor z-10 light:cm-light dark:cm-light flex h-full w-full flex-col items-stretch ͼk ͼy"><div class="cm-scroller"><div class="cm-content q9tKkq_readonly"><span class="ͼn">WITH</span><span> hourly_sales </span><span class="ͼn">AS</span><span> (</span><br><span>    </span><span class="ͼn">SELECT</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">*</span><span>,</span><br><span>        </span><span class="ͼn">CASE</span><span> </span><br><span>            </span><span class="ͼn">WHEN</span><span> EXTRACT(</span><span class="ͼn">HOUR</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">FROM</span><span> sale_time) </span><span class="ͼn">&lt;</span><span> </span><span class="ͼq">12</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">THEN</span><span> </span><span class="ͼr">'Morning'</span><br><span>            </span><span class="ͼn">WHEN</span><span> EXTRACT(</span><span </span><span class="ͼn">FROM</span><span> retail_sales</span><br><span>)</span><br><span class="ͼn">SELECT</span><span> shift,</span><br><span>       </span><span class="ͼn">COUNT</span><span>(</span><span class="ͼn">*</span><span>) </span><span class="ͼn">AS</span><span> total_orders</span><br><span class="ͼn">FROM</span><span> hourly_sales</span><br><span <h1 data-start="305" data-end="348">🛒 Retail Sales SQL Data Analysis Project</h1>
<h2 data-start="350" data-end="372">📌 Project Overview</h2>
<p data-start="374" data-end="521">This project analyzes retail sales data using SQL.<br data-start="424" data-end="427">
The goal is to clean the dataset and answer key business questions to generate insights about:</p>
<ul data-start="523" data-end="610">
<li data-start="523" data-end="544">
<p data-start="525" data-end="544">Sales performance</p>
</li>
<li data-start="545" data-end="566">
<p data-start="547" data-end="566">Customer behavior</p>
</li>
<li data-start="567" data-end="591">
<p data-start="569" data-end="591">Category performance</p>
</li>
<li data-start="592" data-end="610">
<p data-start="594" data-end="610">Monthly trends</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="612" data-end="697">This project demonstrates real-world SQL skills required for a <strong data-start="675" data-end="696">Data Analyst role</strong>.</p>
<hr data-start="699" data-end="702">
<h2 data-start="704" data-end="729">🗂 Dataset Information</h2>
<p data-start="731" data-end="761"><strong data-start="731" data-end="746">Table Name:</strong> <code data-start="747" data-end="761">retail_sales</code></p>
<h3 data-start="763" data-end="785">📊 Table Structure</h3>
<div class="TyagGW_tableContainer"><div tabindex="-1" class="group TyagGW_tableWrapper flex flex-col-reverse w-fit"><table data-start="787" data-end="1200" class="w-fit min-w-(--thread-content-width)"><thead data-start="787" data-end="820"><tr data-start="787" data-end="820"><th data-start="787" data-end="807" data-col-size="sm" class="">Column Name</th><th data-start="807" data-end="820" data-col-size="sm" class="">Data Type</th></tr></thead><tbody data-start="855" data-end="1200"><tr data-start="855" data-end="896"><td data-start="855" data-end="875" data-col-size="sm">transactions_id</td><td data-start="875" data-end="896" data-col-size="sm">INT (Primary Key)</td></tr><tr data-start="897" data-end="925"><td data-start="897" data-end="917" data-col-size="sm">sale_date</td><td data-start="917" data-end="925" data-col-size="sm">DATE</td></tr><tr data-start="926" data-end="954"><td data-start="926" data-end="946" data-col-size="sm">sale_time</td><td data-start="946" data-end="954" data-col-size="sm">TIME</td></tr><tr data-start="955" data-end="982"><td data-start="955" data-end="975" <h2 data-start="2203" data-end="2234">Q3️⃣ Total Sales by Category</h2>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="2236" data-end="2357"><div class="relative w-full mt-4 mb-1"><div class=""><div class="relative"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0" style="width: 100%; margin-bottom: calc(-4px); height: calc(4px); mask-image: linear-gradient(transparent 25%, white 75%);"><div class="sticky bg-token-border-light" style="top: calc(var(--sticky-padding-top) + 48px); height: 1px;"></div></div></div><div class="" style="transform: none;"><div class="relative z-0 flex max-w-full"><div id="code-block-viewer" dir="ltr" class="q9tKkq_viewer cm-editor z-10 light:cm-light dark:cm-light flex h-full w-full flex-col items-stretch ͼk ͼy"><div class="cm-scroller"><div class="cm-content q9tKkq_readonly"><span class="ͼn">SELECT</span><span> category,</span><br><span>       SUM(total_sale) </span><span class="ͼn">AS</span><span> total_sale</span><br><span class="ͼn">FROM</span><span> retail_sales</span><br><span class="ͼn">GROUP</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">BY</span><span> category</span><br><span class="ͼn">ORDER</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">BY</span><span> total_sale;</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=""><div class="" style="width: 100%; <h2 data-start="2364" data-end="2401">Q4️⃣ Average Age (Beauty Category)</h2>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="2403" data-end="2494"><div class="relative w-full mt-4 mb-1"><div class=""><div class="relative"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0" style="width: 100%; <h2 data-start="2823" data-end="2880">Q7️⃣ Best Selling Month in Each Year (Window Function)</h2>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="2882" data-end="3270"><div class="relative w-full mt-4 mb-1"><div class=""><div class="relative"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0"><div class="h-full absolute inset-x-4 top-12 bottom-4"><div class="pointer-events-none sticky z-40 shrink-0 z-1!" style="top: calc(calc(var(--sticky-padding-top) + 48px) - 1px * 3); margin-bottom: calc(-4px); height: calc(4px); mask-image: linear-gradient(transparent 25%, white 75%);"><div class="sticky bg-token-border-light" style="top: calc(var(--sticky-padding-top) + 48px); height: 1px;"></div></div></div><div class="" style="transform: none;"><div class="relative z-0 flex max-w-full"><div id="code-block-viewer" dir="ltr" class="q9tKkq_viewer cm-editor z-10 light:cm-light dark:cm-light flex h-full w-full flex-col items-stretch ͼk ͼy"><div class="cm-scroller"><div class="cm-content q9tKkq_readonly"><span class="ͼn">SELECT</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">*</span><br><span class="ͼn">FROM</span><span> (</span><br><span>    </span><span class="ͼn">SELECT</span><span> EXTRACT(</span><span class="ͼn">YEAR</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">FROM</span><span> sale_date) </span><span class="ͼn">AS</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">year</span><span>,</span><br><span>           EXTRACT(</span><span class="ͼn">MONTH</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">FROM</span><span> sale_date) </span><span class="ͼn">AS</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">month</span><span>,</span><br><span>           AVG(total_sale) </span><span class="ͼn">AS</span><span> average_sale,</span><br><span>           RANK() OVER (</span><br><span>               PARTITION </span><span class="ͼn">BY</span><span> EXTRACT(</span><span AVG(total_sale) </span><span class="ͼn">DESC</span><br><span>           ) </span><span class="ͼn">AS</span><span> rank</span><br><span>    </span><span class="ͼn">FROM</span><span> retail_sales</span><br><span>    </span><span class="ͼn">GROUP</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">BY</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">year</span><span>, </span><span class="ͼn">month</span><br><span>) </span><span class="ͼn">AS</span><span> t</span><br><span class="ͼn">WHERE</span><span> rank </span><span class="ͼn">=</span><span> </span><span class="ͼq">1</span><span>;</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=""><div class="" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"></div></div></div></div></div></pre>

margin-bottom: calc(-4px); height: calc(4px); mask-image: linear-gradient(transparent 25%, white 75%);"><div class="sticky bg-token-border-light" style="top: calc(var(--sticky-padding-top) + 48px); height: 1px;"></div></div></div><div class="" style="transform: none;"><div class="relative z-0 flex max-w-full"><div id="code-block-viewer" dir="ltr" class="q9tKkq_viewer cm-editor z-10 light:cm-light dark:cm-light flex h-full w-full flex-col items-stretch ͼk ͼy"><div class="cm-scroller"><div class="cm-content q9tKkq_readonly"><span class="ͼn">SELECT</span><span> customer_id,</span><br><span>       SUM(total_sale) </span><span class="ͼn">AS</span><span> total_sale</span><br><span class="ͼn">FROM</span><span> retail_sales</span><br><span class="ͼn">GROUP</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">BY</span><span> customer_id</span><br><span class="ͼn">ORDER</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">BY</span><span> total_sale </span><span class="ͼn">DESC</span><br><span class="ͼn">LIMIT</span><span> </span><span class="ͼq">5</span><span>;</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=""><div class="" style="width: 100%; <h2 data-start="3464" data-end="3500">Q9️⃣ Unique Customers by Category</h2>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="3502" data-end="3620"><div class="relative w-full mt-4 mb-1"><div class=""><div class="relative"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0" style="width: 100%; <h2 data-start="3627" data-end="3661">Q🔟 Sales by Shift (CTE + CASE)</h2>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="3663" data-end="4023"><div class="relative w-full mt-4 mb-1"><div class=""><div class="relative"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"><div class="border border-token-border-light border-radius-3xl corner-superellipse/1.1 rounded-3xl"><div class="h-full w-full border-radius-3xl bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary corner-superellipse/1.1 overflow-clip rounded-3xl lxnfua_clipPathFallback"><div class="sticky z-2 select-none top-(--sticky-padding-top)"><div class="flex w-full items-center justify-between py-1.5 ps-4 pe-1.5 font-sans md:ps-5 bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary"><div class="flex max-w-[75%] min-w-0 cursor-default items-center text-sm font-medium justify-self-start text-token-text-primary"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm me-2.5 shrink-0"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-fk4oovux.svg#e45ab3" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>SQL</div><div class="flex flex-row items-center gap-0.5 justify-self-end"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-2 text-sm font-medium hover:bg-black/5 dark:hover:bg-white/10 size-9 rounded-full px-2" aria-label="Copy" data-state="closed"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-md"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-fk4oovux.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg></button></div></div></div><div class="pointer-events-none absolute inset-x-4 top-12 bottom-4"><div class="pointer-events-none sticky z-40 shrink-0 z-1!" style="top: calc(calc(var(--sticky-padding-top) + 48px) - 1px * 3); margin-bottom: calc(-4px); height: calc(4px); mask-image: linear-gradient(transparent 25%, white 75%);"><div class="sticky bg-token-border-light" style="top: calc(var(--sticky-padding-top) + 48px); height: 1px;"></div></div></div><div class="" style="transform: none;"><div class="relative z-0 flex max-w-full"><div id="code-block-viewer" dir="ltr" class="q9tKkq_viewer cm-editor z-10 light:cm-light dark:cm-light flex h-full w-full flex-col items-stretch ͼk ͼy"><div class="cm-scroller"><div class="cm-content q9tKkq_readonly"><span class="ͼn">WITH</span><span> hourly_sales </span><span class="ͼn">AS</span><span> (</span><br><span>    </span><span class="ͼn">SELECT</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">*</span><span>,</span><br><span>        </span><span class="ͼn">CASE</span><span> </span><br><span>            </span><span class="ͼn">WHEN</span><span> EXTRACT(</span><span class="ͼn">HOUR</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">FROM</span><span> sale_time) </span><span class="ͼn">&lt;</span><span> </span><span class="ͼq">12</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">THEN</span><span> </span><span class="ͼr">'Morning'</span><br><span>            </span><span class="ͼn">WHEN</span><span> EXTRACT(</span><span class="ͼn">HOUR</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">FROM</span><span> sale_time) </span><span class="ͼn">BETWEEN</span><span> </span><span class="ͼq">12</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">AND</span><span> </span><span class="ͼq">17</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">THEN</span><span> </span><span class="ͼr">'Afternoon'</span><br><span>            </span><span class="ͼn">ELSE</span><span> </span><span class="ͼr">'Evening'</span><br><span>        </span><span class="ͼn">END</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">AS</span><span> shift</span><br><span>    </span><span class="ͼn">FROM</span><span> retail_sales</span><br><span>)</span><br><span class="ͼn">SELECT</span><span> shift,</span><br><span>       </span><span class="ͼn">COUNT</span><span>(</span><span class="ͼn">*</span><span>) </span><span class="ͼn">AS</span><span> total_orders</span><br><span class="ͼn">FROM</span><span> hourly_sales</span><br><span class="ͼn">GROUP</span><span> </span><span class="ͼn">BY</span><span> shift;</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=""><div class="" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"></div></div></div></div></div></pre>

scroll-mt-(--header-height)" tabindex="-1" dir="auto" data-turn-id="e31450be-3adb-468a-bd7c-50ff502ba205" data-testid="conversation-turn-9" data-scroll-anchor="false" data-turn="user"><h5 class="sr-only select-none">You said:</h5><div class="text-base my-auto mx-auto pt-12 [--thread-content-margin:var(--thread-content-margin-xs,calc(var(--spacing)*4))] @w-sm/main:[--thread-content-margin:var(--thread-content-margin-sm,calc(var(--spacing)*6))] @w-lg/main:[--thread-content-margin:var(--thread-content-margin-lg,calc(var(--spacing)*16))] px-(--thread-content-margin)"><div tabindex="-1" class="[--thread-content-max-width:40rem] @w-lg/main:[--thread-content-max-width:48rem] mx-auto max-w-(--thread-content-max-width) flex-1 group/turn-messages focus-visible:outline-hidden relative flex w-full min-w-0 flex-col"><div class="flex max-w-full flex-col gap-4 grow"><div data-message-author-role="user" data-message-id="e31450be-3adb-468a-bd7c-50ff502ba205" dir="auto" class="min-h-8 text-message relative flex w-full flex-col items-end gap-2 text-start break-words whitespace-normal [.text-message+&amp;]:mt-1"><div class="flex w-full flex-col gap-1 empty:hidden items-end rtl:items-start"><div class="user-message-bubble-color corner-superellipse/0.98 relative rounded-[22px] px-4 py-2.5 leading-6 max-w-(--user-chat-width,70%)"><div class="whitespace-pre-wrap">SELECT *
FROM books;

SELECT *
FROM branch;

SELECT *
FROM employees;

SELECT *
FROM issued_status;

SELECT * 
FROM return_status;


SELECT * FROM members ORDER BY member_id;

---REQUIRMENTS


--1 Create a New Book Record -- "978-1-60129-456-2', 'To Kill a Mockingbird', 'Classic', 6.00, 'yes', 'Harper Lee', 'J.B. Lippincott &amp; Co.')"

INSERT INTO books(
book_id,book_title,category,rental_price,status,author,publisher
)
VALUES('978-1-60129-456-2', 'To Kill a Mockingbird', 'Classic', 6.00, 'yes', 'Harper Lee', 'J.B. Lippincott &amp; Co.');

--2 Update an Existing Member's Address
UPDATE members
SET member_address = '125 Main St'
WHERE  member_id = 'C101';
--CHECK
SELECT * FROM members ORDER BY member_id;


--3 Delete a Record from the Issued Status Table 
-- Delete the record with issued_id = 'IS121' from the issued_status table.

DELETE FROM issued_status
WHERE  issued_id  = 'IS121';

--4:Select all books issued by the employee with emp_id = 'E101'.
SELECT issued_emp_id,
	   issued_id,
	   issued_book_id,
	   issued_book_name,
	   issued_date
FROM issued_status
WHERE issued_emp_id = 'E101';

--5: List Members Who Have Issued More Than One Book

SELECT s.issued_member_id,
	   m.member_name
FROM issued_status s
JOIN members m
ON m.member_id = s.issued_member_id
GROUP BY s.issued_member_id,m.member_name
HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT issued_book_id) &gt;1;


--6: Create Summary Tables: Used CTAS to generate new tables based on query results - each book and total book_issued_cnt**
CREATE TABLE books_summary
AS
SELECT 
	 b.book_id,
	 b.book_title,
	 COUNT(s.issued_id) AS no_of_issues
FROM books b
JOIN issued_status s
ON s.issued_book_id = b.book_id
GROUP BY b.book_id,b.book_title;

--7. Retrieve All Books in a Specific Category 'Classic':

SELECT *
FROM books
WHERE category = 'Classic';

--8: Find Total Rental Income by Category
WITH category_rent AS (
    SELECT 
        category,
        SUM(rental_price) AS total_rent
    FROM books
    GROUP BY category
)
SELECT 
    b.category,
    COUNT(s.issued_id) AS no_of_books,
    c.total_rent,
    COUNT(s.issued_id) * c.total_rent AS revenue
FROM issued_status s
JOIN books b
ON b.book_id = s.issued_book_id
JOIN category_rent c
ON b.category = c.category
GROUP BY b.category, c.total_rent;

-- 9. List Members Who Registered in the Last 180 Days
SELECT * 
FROM members
WHERE reg_date &gt;= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL '180 days';


--10 List Employees with Their Branch Manager's Name and their branch details
SELECT e.emp_id,
	   e.emp_name,
	   b.manager_id,
	   b.branch_id,
	   b.branch_address
FROM employees e
JOIN branch b
ON e.branch_id = b.branch_id; 



-- Task 11. Create a Table of Books with Rental Price Above a Certain Threshold 7USD:
CREATE TABLE books_price_greater_than_seven
AS    
SELECT * FROM books
WHERE rental_price &gt; 7

SELECT * FROM 
books_price_greater_than_seven;


-- 12: Retrieve the List of Books Not Yet Returned
SELECT DISTINCT * 
FROM issued_status S
LEFT JOIN  return_status r
ON r.return_id = s.issued_id
WHERE r.return_id IS NULL;

-- 13 
--Write a query to identify members who have overdue books (assume a 700-day return period). 
--Display the member's_id, member's name, book title, issue date, and days overdue.

SELECT 
	s.issued_member_id,
	m.member_name,
	b.book_title,
	s.issued_date,
	--r.return_date,
	CURRENT_DATE - s.issued_date AS over_due
FROM issued_status s
JOIN members m
ON m.member_id = s.issued_member_id
JOIN books b
ON b.book_id = s.issued_book_id
LEFT JOIN return_status r
ON r.issued_id = s.issued_id
WHERE r.return_date IS NULL
AND CURRENT_DATE - s.issued_date &gt;700
ORDER BY 1;

--
/*
14: Branch Performance Report
Create a query that generates a performance report for each branch,
showing the number of books issued,the number of books returned, and the total revenue generated from book rentals.
*/
--

SELECT * FROM books;
SELECT * FROM branch;
SELECT * FROM employees;
SELECT * FROM issued_status;
SELECT * FROM return_status;
SELECT * FROM members;

--CREATING A REVENUE TABLE
CREATE TABLE book_revenue AS 
		(SELECT  
		    br.branch_id,
		    br.manager_id,
		    COUNT(s.issued_id) AS books_issued,
		    SUM(b.rental_price) AS total_revenue
		FROM issued_status s
		JOIN employees e
		    ON e.emp_id = s.issued_emp_id
		JOIN branch br
		    ON e.branch_id = br.branch_id
		LEFT JOIN return_status r
		    ON r.issued_id = s.issued_id
		JOIN books b
		    ON s.issued_book_id = b.book_id
		GROUP BY 
		    br.branch_id,
		    br.manager_id
);

 --15 create a new table active_members containing members who have 
 --issued at least one book in the last 2 months.

CREATE TABLE active_members
AS
SELECT * FROM members
WHERE member_id IN (SELECT 
                        DISTINCT issued_member_id   
                    FROM issued_status
                    WHERE 
                        issued_date &gt;= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL '2 month'
                    )
;
SELECT * FROM active_members;


--16: Find Employees with the Most Book Issues Processed
-- Write a query to find the top 3 employees who have processed the most book issues. 
--Display the employee name, number of books processed, and their branch.

SELECT 
    e.emp_name,
    b.*,
    COUNT(s.issued_id) as no_book_issued
FROM issued_status s
JOIN
employees  e
ON e.emp_id = s.issued_emp_id
JOIN
branch  b
ON e.branch_id = b.branch_id
GROUP BY 1, 2
ORDER BY  COUNT(s.issued_id) DESC
LIMIT 3;</div></div></div></div></div><div class="z-0 flex justify-end"><div class="touch:-me-2 touch:-ms-3.5 -ms-2.5 -me-1 flex flex-wrap items-center gap-y-4 p-1 select-none focus-within:transition-none hover:transition-none touch:pointer-events-auto touch:opacity-100 duration-300 group-hover/turn-messages:delay-300 pointer-events-none opacity-0 motion-safe:transition-opacity group-hover/turn-messages:pointer-events-auto group-hover/turn-messages:opacity-100 group-focus-within/turn-messages:pointer-events-auto <hr data-start="312" data-end="315">
<h1 data-start="317" data-end="375">📚 Library Management System – SQL Data Analysis Project</h1>
<h2 data-start="377" data-end="399">📌 Project Overview</h2>
<p data-start="400" data-end="640">This project simulates a <strong data-start="425" data-end="454">Library Management System</strong> using SQL. It demonstrates how relational databases can be used to manage and analyze library operations such as book rentals, member activity, employee performance, and branch revenue.</p>
<p data-start="642" data-end="768">The project focuses on solving real-world business questions using <strong data-start="709" data-end="767">SQL queries, joins, aggregations, CTEs, and subqueries</strong>.</p>
<hr data-start="770" data-end="773">
<h1 data-start="775" data-end="799">🎯 Business Objectives</h1>
<p data-start="801" data-end="855">The project answers key operational questions such as:</p>
<ul data-start="857" data-end="1056">
<li data-start="857" data-end="898">
<p data-start="859" data-end="898">Which books are issued most frequently?</p>
</li>
<li data-start="899" data-end="931">
<p data-start="901" data-end="931">Which members are most active?</p>
</li>
<li data-start="932" data-end="979">
<p data-start="934" data-end="979">Which employees process the most book issues?</p>
</li>
<li data-start="980" data-end="1029">
<p data-start="982" data-end="1029">Which branch generates the most rental revenue?</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1030" data-end="1056">
<p data-start="1032" data-end="1056">Which books are overdue?</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="1058" data-end="1154">These insights help library management <strong data-start="1097" data-end="1154">improve operational efficiency and track performance.</strong></p>
<hr data-start="1156" data-end="1159">
<h1 data-start="1161" data-end="1181">🗂 Database Schema</h1>
<h3 data-start="1183" data-end="1198">Tables Used</h3>
<div class="TyagGW_tableContainer"><div tabindex="-1" class="group TyagGW_tableWrapper flex flex-col-reverse w-fit"><table data-start="1200" data-end="1485" class="w-fit min-w-(--thread-content-width)"><thead data-start="1200" data-end="1223"><tr data-start="1200" data-end="1223"><th data-start="1200" data-end="1208" data-col-size="sm" class="">Table</th><th data-start="1208" data-end="1223" data-col-size="sm" class="">Description</th></tr></thead><tbody data-start="1247" data-end="1485"><tr data-start="1247" data-end="1288"><td data-start="1247" data-end="1255" data-col-size="sm">books</td><td data-start="1255" data-end="1288" data-col-size="sm">Contains all book information</td></tr><tr data-start="1289" data-end="1329"><td data-start="1289" data-end="1299" data-col-size="sm">members</td><td data-start="1299" data-end="1329" data-col-size="sm">Registered library members</td></tr><tr data-start="1330" data-end="1363"><td data-start="1330" data-end="1342" data-col-size="sm">employees</td><td data-start="1342" data-end="1363" data-col-size="sm">Library employees</td></tr><tr data-start="1364" data-end="1395"><td data-start="1364" data-end="1373" data-col-size="sm">branch</td><td data-start="1373" data-end="1395" data-col-size="sm">Branch information</td></tr><tr data-start="1396" data-end="1439"><td data-start="1396" data-end="1412" data-col-size="sm">issued_status</td><td data-start="1412" data-end="1439" data-col-size="sm">Records of issued books</td></tr><tr data-start="1440" data-end="1485"><td data-start="1440" data-end="1456" data-col-size="sm">return_status</td><td data-start="1456" data-end="1485" data-col-size="sm">Records of returned books</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="sticky <hr data-start="1487" data-end="1490">
<h1 data-start="1492" data-end="1522">🧠 Entity Relationship Logic</h1>
<p data-start="1524" data-end="1577">The system works through the following relationships:</p>
<ul data-start="1579" data-end="1713">
<li data-start="1579" data-end="1607">
<p data-start="1581" data-end="1607"><strong data-start="1581" data-end="1607">Members → Issued Books</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-start="1608" data-end="1645">
<p data-start="1610" data-end="1645"><strong data-start="1610" data-end="1645">Employees → Process Book Issues</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-start="1646" data-end="1679">
<p data-start="1648" data-end="1679"><strong data-start="1648" data-end="1679">Branches → Employ Employees</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-start="1680" data-end="1713">
<p data-start="1682" data-end="1713"><strong data-start="1682" data-end="1713">Books → Issued and Returned</strong></p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="1715" data-end="1737">Example relationships:</p>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="1739" data-end="1978"><div class="relative w-full mt-4 mb-1"><div class=""><div class="relative"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"><div class="border border-token-border-light border-radius-3xl corner-superellipse/1.1 rounded-3xl"><div class="h-full w-full border-radius-3xl bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary corner-superellipse/1.1 overflow-clip rounded-3xl lxnfua_clipPathFallback"><div class="pointer-events-none absolute end-1.5 top-1 z-2 md:end-2 md:top-1"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none pointer-events-auto py-2 text-sm font-medium hover:bg-black/5 dark:hover:bg-white/10 size-9 rounded-full px-2" aria-label="Copy" data-state="closed"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-md"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-fk4oovux.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg></button></div><div class="pe-11 pt-3" style="transform: none;"><div class="relative z-0 flex max-w-full"><div id="code-block-viewer" dir="ltr" class="q9tKkq_viewer cm-editor z-10 light:cm-light dark:cm-light flex h-full w-full flex-col items-stretch ͼk ͼy"><div class="cm-scroller"><div class="cm-content q9tKkq_readonly"><span>members.member_id → issued_status.issued_member_id</span><br><span>employees.emp_id → issued_status.issued_emp_id</span><br><span>books.book_id → issued_status.issued_book_id</span><br><span>issued_status.issued_id → return_status.issued_id</span><br><span>employees.branch_id → branch.branch_id</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=""><div class="" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"></div></div></div></div></div></pre>

<h1 data-start="3381" data-end="3396">🎯 Conclusion</h1>
<p data-start="3398" data-end="3601">This project demonstrates how SQL can be used to <strong data-start="3447" data-end="3511">manage and analyze operational data in a library environment</strong>. It highlights practical skills in querying, data manipulation, and analytical reporting.</p>

<p data-start="236" data-end="397">For <strong data-start="240" data-end="250">GitHub</strong>, the best practice is to <strong data-start="276" data-end="306">export the ERD as an image</strong> and show it in your README. The <code data-start="339" data-end="347">.pgerd</code> file itself usually can't be previewed on GitHub.</p>
<hr data-start="399" data-end="402">
<h1 data-start="404" data-end="424">What You Should Do</h1>
<h3 data-start="426" data-end="460">1️⃣ Export the ERD as an Image</h3>
<p data-start="462" data-end="477">In <strong data-start="465" data-end="476">pgAdmin</strong>:</p>
<ol data-start="479" data-end="554">
<li data-start="479" data-end="495">
<p data-start="482" data-end="495">Open your ERD</p>
</li>
<li data-start="496" data-end="515">
<p data-start="499" data-end="515">Click <strong data-start="505" data-end="515">Export</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-start="516" data-end="540">
<p data-start="519" data-end="540">Choose <strong data-start="526" data-end="540">PNG or JPG</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-start="541" data-end="554">
<p data-start="544" data-end="554">Save it as</p>
</li>
</ol>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="556" data-end="579"><div class="relative w-full mt-4 mb-1"><div class=""><div class="relative"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"><div class="border border-token-border-light border-radius-3xl corner-superellipse/1.1 rounded-3xl"><div class="h-full w-full border-radius-3xl bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary corner-superellipse/1.1 overflow-clip rounded-3xl lxnfua_clipPathFallback"><div class="pointer-events-none absolute end-1.5 top-1 z-2 md:end-2 md:top-1"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none pointer-events-auto py-2 text-sm font-medium hover:bg-black/5 dark:hover:bg-white/10 size-9 rounded-full px-2" aria-label="Copy" data-state="closed"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-md"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-fk4oovux.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg></button></div><div class="pe-11 pt-3" style="transform: none;"><div class="relative z-0 flex max-w-full"><div id="code-block-viewer" dir="ltr" class="q9tKkq_viewer cm-editor z-10 light:cm-light dark:cm-light flex h-full w-full flex-col items-stretch ͼk ͼy"><div class="cm-scroller"><div class="cm-content q9tKkq_readonly"><span>library_erd.png</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=""><div class="" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"></div></div></div></div></div></pre>

<p data-start="1751" data-end="1773">Tracks returned books.</p>
<p data-start="1775" data-end="1787">Primary Key:</p>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="1788" data-end="1805"><div class="relative w-full mt-4 mb-1"><div class=""><div class="relative"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"><div class="border border-token-border-light border-radius-3xl corner-superellipse/1.1 rounded-3xl"><div class="h-full w-full border-radius-3xl bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary corner-superellipse/1.1 overflow-clip rounded-3xl lxnfua_clipPathFallback"><div class="pointer-events-none absolute end-1.5 top-1 z-2 md:end-2 md:top-1"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none pointer-events-auto py-2 text-sm font-medium hover:bg-black/5 dark:hover:bg-white/10 size-9 rounded-full px-2" aria-label="Copy" data-state="closed"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-md"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-fk4oovux.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg></button></div><div class="pe-11 pt-3" style="transform: none;"><div class="relative z-0 flex max-w-full"><div id="code-block-viewer" dir="ltr" class="q9tKkq_viewer cm-editor z-10 light:cm-light dark:cm-light flex h-full w-full flex-col items-stretch ͼk ͼy"><div class="cm-scroller"><div class="cm-content q9tKkq_readonly"><span>return_id</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=""><div class="" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"></div></div></div></div></div></pre>
<p data-start="1807" data-end="1819">Foreign Key:</p>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="1820" data-end="1863"><div class="relative w-full mt-4 mb-1"><div class=""><div class="relative"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"><div class="border border-token-border-light border-radius-3xl corner-superellipse/1.1 rounded-3xl"><div class="h-full w-full border-radius-3xl bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary corner-superellipse/1.1 overflow-clip rounded-3xl lxnfua_clipPathFallback"><div class="pointer-events-none absolute end-1.5 top-1 z-2 md:end-2 md:top-1"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none pointer-events-auto py-2 text-sm font-medium hover:bg-black/5 dark:hover:bg-white/10 size-9 rounded-full px-2" aria-label="Copy" data-state="closed"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-md"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-fk4oovux.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg></button></div><div class="pe-11 pt-3" style="transform: none;"><div class="relative z-0 flex max-w-full"><div id="code-block-viewer" dir="ltr" class="q9tKkq_viewer cm-editor z-10 light:cm-light dark:cm-light flex h-full w-full flex-col items-stretch ͼk ͼy"><div class="cm-scroller"><div class="cm-content q9tKkq_readonly"><span>issued_id → issued_status.issued_id</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=""><div class="" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"></div></div></div></div></div></pre>

<hr data-start="153" data-end="156">
<h1 data-start="158" data-end="190">📚 Database Table Descriptions</h1>
<h2 data-start="192" data-end="210">1️⃣ Books Table</h2>
<p data-start="211" data-end="401">The <strong data-start="215" data-end="224">books</strong> table stores information about all books available in the library.<br data-start="291" data-end="294">
It includes details such as book title, category, author, publisher, rental price, and availability status.</p>
<p data-start="403" data-end="418"><strong data-start="403" data-end="418">Key Columns</strong></p>
<ul data-start="419" data-end="737">
<li data-start="419" data-end="478">
<p data-start="421" data-end="478"><code data-start="421" data-end="430">book_id</code> – Unique identifier for each book (Primary Key)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="479" data-end="512">
<p data-start="481" data-end="512"><code data-start="481" data-end="493">book_title</code> – Name of the book</p>
</li>
<li data-start="513" data-end="557">
<p data-start="515" data-end="557"><code data-start="515" data-end="525">category</code> – Genre or category of the book</p>
</li>
<li data-start="558" data-end="611">
<p data-start="560" data-end="611"><code data-start="560" data-end="574">rental_price</code> – Price charged for renting the book</p>
</li>
<li data-start="612" data-end="670">
<p data-start="614" data-end="670"><code data-start="614" data-end="622">status</code> – Availability of the book (available / issued)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="671" data-end="702">
<p data-start="673" data-end="702"><code data-start="673" data-end="681">author</code> – Author of the book</p>
</li>
<li data-start="703" data-end="737">
<p data-start="705" data-end="737"><code data-start="705" data-end="716">publisher</code> – Publishing company</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="739" data-end="742">
<h2 data-start="744" data-end="764">2️⃣ Members Table</h2>
<p data-start="765" data-end="857">The <strong data-start="769" data-end="780">members</strong> table contains information about people who are registered with the library.</p>
<p data-start="859" data-end="874"><strong data-start="859" data-end="874">Key Columns</strong></p>
<ul data-start="875" data-end="1082">
<li data-start="875" data-end="938">
<p data-start="877" data-end="938"><code data-start="877" data-end="888">member_id</code> – Unique identifier for each member (Primary Key)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="939" data-end="975">
<p data-start="941" data-end="975"><code data-start="941" data-end="954">member_name</code> – Name of the member</p>
</li>
<li data-start="976" data-end="1018">
<p data-start="978" data-end="1018"><code data-start="978" data-end="994">member_address</code> – Address of the member</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1019" data-end="1082">
<p data-start="1021" data-end="1082"><code data-start="1021" data-end="1031">reg_date</code> – Date when the member registered with the library</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="1084" data-end="1087">
<h2 data-start="1089" data-end="1111">3️⃣ Employees Table</h2>
<p data-start="1112" data-end="1211">The <strong data-start="1116" data-end="1129">employees</strong> table stores information about library staff who process book issues and returns.</p>
<p data-start="1213" data-end="1228"><strong data-start="1213" data-end="1228">Key Columns</strong></p>
<ul data-start="1229" data-end="1389">
<li data-start="1229" data-end="1291">
<p data-start="1231" data-end="1291"><code data-start="1231" data-end="1239">emp_id</code> – Unique identifier for each employee (Primary Key)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1292" data-end="1327">
<p data-start="1294" data-end="1327"><code data-start="1294" data-end="1304">emp_name</code> – Name of the employee</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1328" data-end="1389">
<p data-start="1330" data-end="1389"><code data-start="1330" data-end="1341">branch_id</code> – Branch where the employee works (Foreign Key)</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="1391" data-end="1394">
<h2 data-start="1396" data-end="1415">4️⃣ Branch Table</h2>
<p data-start="1416" data-end="1485">The <strong data-start="1420" data-end="1430">branch</strong> table stores details about different library branches.</p>
<p data-start="1487" data-end="1502"><strong data-start="1487" data-end="1502">Key Columns</strong></p>
<ul data-start="1503" data-end="1658">
<li data-start="1503" data-end="1566">
<p data-start="1505" data-end="1566"><code data-start="1505" data-end="1516">branch_id</code> – Unique identifier for each branch (Primary Key)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1567" data-end="1609">
<p data-start="1569" data-end="1609"><code data-start="1569" data-end="1585">branch_address</code> – Address of the branch</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1610" data-end="1658">
<p data-start="1612" data-end="1658"><code data-start="1612" data-end="1624">manager_id</code> – Employee who manages the branch</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="1660" data-end="1663">
<h2 data-start="1665" data-end="1691">5️⃣ Issued Status Table</h2>
<p data-start="1692" data-end="1755">The <strong data-start="1696" data-end="1713">issued_status</strong> table tracks all book issue transactions.</p>
<p data-start="1757" data-end="1772"><strong data-start="1757" data-end="1772">Key Columns</strong></p>
<ul data-start="1773" data-end="2079">
<li data-start="1773" data-end="1847">
<p data-start="1775" data-end="1847"><code data-start="1775" data-end="1786">issued_id</code> – Unique identifier for each issue transaction (Primary Key)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1848" data-end="1913">
<p data-start="1850" data-end="1913"><code data-start="1850" data-end="1868">issued_member_id</code> – Member who borrowed the book (Foreign Key)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1914" data-end="1969">
<p data-start="1916" data-end="1969"><code data-start="1916" data-end="1932">issued_book_id</code> – Book that was issued (Foreign Key)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1970" data-end="2036">
<p data-start="1972" data-end="2036"><code data-start="1972" data-end="1987">issued_emp_id</code> – Employee who processed the issue (Foreign Key)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="2037" data-end="2079">
<p data-start="2039" data-end="2079"><code data-start="2039" data-end="2052">issued_date</code> – Date the book was issued</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="2081" data-end="2084">
<h2 data-start="2086" data-end="2112">6️⃣ Return Status Table</h2>
<p data-start="2113" data-end="2178">The <strong data-start="2117" data-end="2134">return_status</strong> table tracks books that have been returned.</p>
<p data-start="2180" data-end="2195"><strong data-start="2180" data-end="2195">Key Columns</strong></p>
<ul data-start="2196" data-end="2432">
<li data-start="2196" data-end="2266">
<p data-start="2198" data-end="2266"><code data-start="2198" data-end="2209">return_id</code> – Unique identifier for each return record (Primary Key)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="2267" data-end="2332">
<p data-start="2269" data-end="2332"><code data-start="2269" data-end="2280">issued_id</code> – Reference to the issued transaction (Foreign Key)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="2333" data-end="2377">
<p data-start="2335" data-end="2377"><code data-start="2335" data-end="2348">return_date</code> – Date the book was returned</p>
</li>
<li data-start="2378" data-end="2432">
<p data-start="2380" data-end="2432"><code data-start="2380" data-end="2394">book_quality</code> – Condition of the book when returned</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="2434" data-end="2437">
<p data-start="2439" data-end="2473">💡 <strong data-start="2442" data-end="2473">Tip for your GitHub project</strong></p>
<p data-start="2475" data-end="2517">After the <strong data-start="2485" data-end="2498">ERD image</strong>, add this section:</p>

leading-6 max-w-(--user-chat-width,70%)"><div class="whitespace-pre-wrap">remake this considering this also
--Project Library Management System
--Create tables
--Branch Table
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS branch;
CREATE TABLE branch(
			branch_id VARCHAR(50) PRIMARY KEY,
			manager_id VARCHAR(50),
			branch_address VARCHAR(50),
			contact_no  VARCHAR(20)

);

--employee table
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS employees;
CREATE TABLE employees (
			 emp_id VARCHAR(20) PRIMARY KEY,
			 emp_name VARCHAR(20),
			 position VARCHAR(20),
			 salary INT,
			 branch_id VARCHAR(20) --FK

);

--books table
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS books;
CREATE TABLE books (
			book_id VARCHAR(20) PRIMARY KEY,
			book_title VARCHAR(75),
			category VARCHAR(10),
			rental_price FLOAT,
			status VARCHAR(15),
			author VARCHAR(50),
			publisher VARCHAR(25)

)
;

---members table
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS members;
CREATE TABLE members (
			member_id VARCHAR(20) PRIMARY KEY,
			member_name VARCHAR(30),
			member_address VARCHAR(75),
			reg_date DATE

);


--issued_statues
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS issued_status;
CREATE TABLE issued_status(
			issued_id VARCHAR(10) PRIMARY KEY,
			issued_member_id VARCHAR(10),--FK
			issued_book_name VARCHAR(75),
			issued_date DATE,
			issued_book_id VARCHAR(25), --FK
			issued_emp_id VARCHAR(10) --FK 

);


--retutrn_status
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS return_status;
CREATE TABLE return_status(
			return_id VARCHAR(10) PRIMARY KEY,
			issued_id VARCHAR(10), --FK
			return_book_name VARCHAR(75),
			return_date DATE,
			return_book_id VARCHAR(20) --FK

);

--FRORIEGN KEY CONSTRAINS
--issued_member_id
ALTER TABLE issued_status
ADD CONSTRAINT fk_members
FOREIGN KEY (issued_member_id)         --which column has a foriegn key
REFERENCES   members(member_id);         --In which table and column member_id is a primary key

--issued_book_id
ALTER TABLE issued_status
ADD CONSTRAINT fk_books
FOREIGN KEY (issued_book_id)     
REFERENCES   books(book_id);        

--issued_emp_id
ALTER TABLE issued_status
ADD CONSTRAINT fk_employees
FOREIGN KEY (issued_emp_id)     
REFERENCES   employees(emp_id);        


--branch_id
ALTER TABLE employees
ADD CONSTRAINT fk_branch
FOREIGN KEY (branch_id)    
REFERENCES	branch(branch_id) ;


--issued_id
ALTER TABLE return_status
ADD CONSTRAINT fk_issued_status
FOREIGN KEY (issued_id)     
REFERENCES   issued_status(issued_id);    

--return_book_id
ALTER TABLE return_status
ADD CONSTRAINT fk_return_book
FOREIGN KEY (return_book_id)     
REFERENCES   books(book_id);   

</div></div></div></div></div><div class="z-0 flex justify-end"><div class="touch:-me-2 touch:-ms-3.5 -ms-2.5 -me-1 flex flex-wrap items-center gap-y-4 p-1 select-none focus-within:transition-none [.text-message+&amp;]:mt-1"><div class="flex w-full flex-col gap-1 empty:hidden items-end rtl:items-start"><div class="user-message-bubble-color corner-superellipse/0.98 relative rounded-[22px] px-4 py-2.5 leading-6 max-w-(--user-chat-width,70%)"><div class="whitespace-pre-wrap">--Project Library Management System
--Create tables
--Branch Table
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS branch;
CREATE TABLE branch(
			branch_id VARCHAR(50) PRIMARY KEY,
			manager_id VARCHAR(50),
			branch_address VARCHAR(50),
			contact_no  VARCHAR(20)

);

--employee table
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS employees;
CREATE TABLE employees (
			 emp_id VARCHAR(20) PRIMARY KEY,
			 emp_name VARCHAR(20),
			 position VARCHAR(20),
			 salary INT,
			 branch_id VARCHAR(20) --FK

);

--books table
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS books;
CREATE TABLE books (
			book_id VARCHAR(20) PRIMARY KEY,
			book_title VARCHAR(75),
			category VARCHAR(10),
			rental_price FLOAT,
			status VARCHAR(15),
			author VARCHAR(50),
			publisher VARCHAR(25)

)
;

---members table
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS members;
CREATE TABLE members (
			member_id VARCHAR(20) PRIMARY KEY,
			member_name VARCHAR(30),
			member_address VARCHAR(75),
			reg_date DATE

);


--issued_statues
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS issued_status;
CREATE TABLE issued_status(
			issued_id VARCHAR(10) PRIMARY KEY,
			issued_member_id VARCHAR(10),--FK
			issued_book_name VARCHAR(75),
			issued_date DATE,
			issued_book_id VARCHAR(25), --FK
			issued_emp_id VARCHAR(10) --FK 

);


--retutrn_status
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS return_status;
CREATE TABLE return_status(
			return_id VARCHAR(10) PRIMARY KEY,
			issued_id VARCHAR(10), --FK
			return_book_name VARCHAR(75),
			return_date DATE,
			return_book_id VARCHAR(20) --FK

);

--FRORIEGN KEY CONSTRAINS
--issued_member_id
ALTER TABLE issued_status
ADD CONSTRAINT fk_members
FOREIGN KEY (issued_member_id)         --which column has a foriegn key
REFERENCES   members(member_id);         --In which table and column member_id is a primary key

--issued_book_id
ALTER TABLE issued_status
ADD CONSTRAINT fk_books
FOREIGN KEY (issued_book_id)     
REFERENCES   books(book_id);        

--issued_emp_id
ALTER TABLE issued_status
ADD CONSTRAINT fk_employees
FOREIGN KEY (issued_emp_id)     
REFERENCES   employees(emp_id);        


--branch_id
ALTER TABLE employees
ADD CONSTRAINT fk_branch
FOREIGN KEY (branch_id)    
REFERENCES	branch(branch_id) ;


--issued_id
ALTER TABLE return_status
ADD CONSTRAINT fk_issued_status
FOREIGN KEY (issued_id)     
REFERENCES   issued_status(issued_id);    

--return_book_id
ALTER TABLE return_status
ADD CONSTRAINT fk_return_book
FOREIGN KEY (return_book_id)     
REFERENCES   books(book_id);   

this is the table creation and erd and the foriegn key making query


SELECT *
FROM books;

SELECT *
FROM branch;

SELECT *
FROM employees;

SELECT *
FROM issued_status;

SELECT * 
FROM return_status;


SELECT * FROM members ORDER BY member_id;

---REQUIRMENTS


--1 Create a New Book Record -- "978-1-60129-456-2', 'To Kill a Mockingbird', 'Classic', 6.00, 'yes', 'Harper Lee', 'J.B. Lippincott &amp; Co.')"

INSERT INTO books(
book_id,book_title,category,rental_price,status,author,publisher
)
VALUES('978-1-60129-456-2', 'To Kill a Mockingbird', 'Classic', 6.00, 'yes', 'Harper Lee', 'J.B. Lippincott &amp; Co.');

--2 Update an Existing Member's Address
UPDATE members
SET member_address = '125 Main St'
WHERE  member_id = 'C101';
--CHECK
SELECT * FROM members ORDER BY member_id;


--3 Delete a Record from the Issued Status Table 
-- Delete the record with issued_id = 'IS121' from the issued_status table.

DELETE FROM issued_status
WHERE  issued_id  = 'IS121';

--4:Select all books issued by the employee with emp_id = 'E101'.
SELECT issued_emp_id,
	   issued_id,
	   issued_book_id,
	   issued_book_name,
	   issued_date
FROM issued_status
WHERE issued_emp_id = 'E101';

--5: List Members Who Have Issued More Than One Book

SELECT s.issued_member_id,
	   m.member_name
FROM issued_status s
JOIN members m
ON m.member_id = s.issued_member_id
GROUP BY s.issued_member_id,m.member_name
HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT issued_book_id) &gt;1;


--6: Create Summary Tables: Used CTAS to generate new tables based on query results - each book and total book_issued_cnt**
CREATE TABLE books_summary
AS
SELECT 
	 b.book_id,
	 b.book_title,
	 COUNT(s.issued_id) AS no_of_issues
FROM books b
JOIN issued_status s
ON s.issued_book_id = b.book_id
GROUP BY b.book_id,b.book_title;

--7. Retrieve All Books in a Specific Category 'Classic':

SELECT *
FROM books
WHERE category = 'Classic';

--8: Find Total Rental Income by Category
WITH category_rent AS (
    SELECT 
        category,
        SUM(rental_price) AS total_rent
    FROM books
    GROUP BY category
)
SELECT 
    b.category,
    COUNT(s.issued_id) AS no_of_books,
    c.total_rent,
    COUNT(s.issued_id) * c.total_rent AS revenue
FROM issued_status s
JOIN books b
ON b.book_id = s.issued_book_id
JOIN category_rent c
ON b.category = c.category
GROUP BY b.category, c.total_rent;

-- 9. List Members Who Registered in the Last 180 Days
SELECT * 
FROM members
WHERE reg_date &gt;= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL '180 days';


--10 List Employees with Their Branch Manager's Name and their branch details
SELECT e.emp_id,
	   e.emp_name,
	   b.manager_id,
	   b.branch_id,
	   b.branch_address
FROM employees e
JOIN branch b
ON e.branch_id = b.branch_id; 



-- Task 11. Create a Table of Books with Rental Price Above a Certain Threshold 7USD:
CREATE TABLE books_price_greater_than_seven
AS    
SELECT * FROM books
WHERE rental_price &gt; 7

SELECT * FROM 
books_price_greater_than_seven;


-- 12: Retrieve the List of Books Not Yet Returned
SELECT DISTINCT * 
FROM issued_status S
LEFT JOIN  return_status r
ON r.return_id = s.issued_id
WHERE r.return_id IS NULL;

-- 13 
--Write a query to identify members who have overdue books (assume a 700-day return period). 
--Display the member's_id, member's name, book title, issue date, and days overdue.

SELECT 
	s.issued_member_id,
	m.member_name,
	b.book_title,
	s.issued_date,
	--r.return_date,
	CURRENT_DATE - s.issued_date AS over_due
FROM issued_status s
JOIN members m
ON m.member_id = s.issued_member_id
JOIN books b
ON b.book_id = s.issued_book_id
LEFT JOIN return_status r
ON r.issued_id = s.issued_id
WHERE r.return_date IS NULL
AND CURRENT_DATE - s.issued_date &gt;700
ORDER BY 1;

--
/*
14: Branch Performance Report
Create a query that generates a performance report for each branch,
showing the number of books issued,the number of books returned, and the total revenue generated from book rentals.
*/
--

SELECT * FROM books;
SELECT * FROM branch;
SELECT * FROM employees;
SELECT * FROM issued_status;
SELECT * FROM return_status;
SELECT * FROM members;

--CREATING A REVENUE TABLE
CREATE TABLE book_revenue AS 
		(SELECT  
		    br.branch_id,
		    br.manager_id,
		    COUNT(s.issued_id) AS books_issued,
		    SUM(b.rental_price) AS total_revenue
		FROM issued_status s
		JOIN employees e
		    ON e.emp_id = s.issued_emp_id
		JOIN branch br
		    ON e.branch_id = br.branch_id
		LEFT JOIN return_status r
		    ON r.issued_id = s.issued_id
		JOIN books b
		    ON s.issued_book_id = b.book_id
		GROUP BY 
		    br.branch_id,
		    br.manager_id
);

 --15 create a new table active_members containing members who have 
 --issued at least one book in the last 2 months.

CREATE TABLE active_members
AS
SELECT * FROM members
WHERE member_id IN (SELECT 
                        DISTINCT issued_member_id   
                    FROM issued_status
                    WHERE 
                        issued_date &gt;= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL '2 month'
                    )
;
SELECT * FROM active_members;


--16: Find Employees with the Most Book Issues Processed
-- Write a query to find the top 3 employees who have processed the most book issues. 
--Display the employee name, number of books processed, and their branch.

SELECT 
    e.emp_name,
    b.*,
    COUNT(s.issued_id) as no_book_issued
FROM issued_status s
JOIN
employees  e
ON e.emp_id = s.issued_emp_id
JOIN
branch  b
ON e.branch_id = b.branch_id
GROUP BY 1, 2
ORDER BY  COUNT(s.issued_id) DESC
LIMIT 3;

<h3 data-start="69" data-end="103">Option 1 (Best – Professional)</h3>
<p data-start="104" data-end="373"><strong data-start="104" data-end="145">Library Management System SQL Project</strong> – A PostgreSQL database project that designs a complete library management system with relational schema, foreign key constraints, and SQL queries to analyze book issues, member activity, branch performance, and rental revenue.</p>
<hr data-start="375" data-end="378">
<h3 data-start="380" data-end="408">Option 2 (Short &amp; Clean)</h3>
<p data-start="409" data-end="559">SQL project that builds a <strong data-start="435" data-end="473">Library Management System database</strong> and solves business problems using joins, CTEs, aggregations, and analytical queries.</p>
<hr data-start="561" data-end="564">
<h3 data-start="566" data-end="612">Option 3 (Best for Data Analyst Portfolio)</h3>
<p data-start="613" data-end="822">A <strong data-start="615" data-end="651">PostgreSQL data analysis project</strong> that models a library database and answers real business questions such as book issuance trends, member activity, overdue books, employee performance, and rental revenue.</p>
<hr data-start="824" data-end="827">
<h3 data-start="829" data-end="869">Option 4 (Very Short – GitHub style)</h3>
<p data-start="870" data-end="968">PostgreSQL project for <strong data-start="893" data-end="967">designing and analyzing a Library Management System database using SQL</strong>.</p>
<hr data-start="970" data-end="973">
<p data-start="975" data-end="1091">✅ <strong data-start="977" data-end="999">My recommendation:</strong> Use <strong data-start="1004" data-end="1016">Option 3</strong> because recruiters like seeing <strong data-start="1048" data-end="1090">"data analysis" + "business questions"</strong>.</p>

<p data-start="598" data-end="668">You can paste this in the <strong data-start="624" data-end="667">repository description or top of README</strong>.</p>

Having</span><br><span>- Subqueries</span><br><span>- Table creation using CTAS</span><br><span>- Date filtering and interval operations</span><br><br><span>This project demonstrates practical SQL skills required for data analysis and database management.</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=""><div class="" style="width: 100%; <p data-start="748" data-end="772"><strong data-start="748" data-end="772">Extended Description</strong></p>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="773" data-end="1833"><div class="relative w-full mt-4 mb-1"><div class=""><div class="relative"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"><div class="border border-token-border-light border-radius-3xl corner-superellipse/1.1 rounded-3xl"><div class="h-full w-full border-radius-3xl bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary corner-superellipse/1.1 overflow-clip rounded-3xl lxnfua_clipPathFallback"><div class="pointer-events-none absolute end-1.5 top-1 z-2 md:end-2 md:top-1"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none pointer-events-auto py-2 text-sm font-medium hover:bg-black/5 dark:hover:bg-white/10 size-9 rounded-full px-2" aria-label="Copy" data-state="closed"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-md"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-fk4oovux.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg></button></div><div class="pe-11 pt-3" style="transform: none;"><div class="relative z-0 flex max-w-full"><div id="code-block-viewer" dir="ltr" class="q9tKkq_viewer cm-editor z-10 light:cm-light dark:cm-light flex h-full w-full flex-col items-stretch ͼk ͼy"><div class="cm-scroller"><div class="cm-content q9tKkq_readonly"><span>This project demonstrates the design and implementation of a Library Management System database using PostgreSQL.</span><br><br><span>The system models core library operations including managing branches, employees, books, members, book issuance, and book returns. The database schema was designed using relational database principles and includes multiple tables connected through foreign key constraints to maintain data integrity.</span><br><br><span>The project also includes a set of SQL queries that solve real-world business problems such as identifying active members, detecting overdue books, analyzing branch performance, and calculating rental revenue generated from book lending activities.</span><br><br><span>Key SQL concepts demonstrated in this project include:</span><br><span>- Database schema design</span><br><span>- Primary and foreign key relationships</span><br><span>- Joins</span><br><span>- Aggregations and Group By</span><br><span>- Common Table Expressions (CTEs)</span><br><span>- Subqueries</span><br><span>- Table creation using CTAS</span><br><span>- Date filtering and interval calculations</span><br><br><span>This project highlights practical SQL skills commonly required for data analysis and database management roles.</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=""><div class="" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"></div></div></div></div></div></pre>
